4     Programming Modes

 

The PP supports two differen t 5X-Programming-Modes but in the DEMO Scenario only the first is supported.

  • 5-X Simultaneous Mode
  • Plane-Mode (FANUC G68.2à FRAME )

 

The corresponding 5X-Mode will be activated with the PP-Word PROGMODE

 

5-X Simultaneous

PROGMODE/5XSIM

 

Plane

PROGMODE/FRAME

 

 

 

Standard: PROGMODE/5XSIM is activated.

 

4.1     5-X Simultaneous Mode

 

This Mode is used fort he 5X-Simultaneous-Machining. One NC-Sentence contain X-, Y-, Z-Coordinates and the two
Rotation Angles A and C. The Data corresponds to the NC-Axis-System.

Application:

  • 5-X Simultaneous Machining
  • 5-X Drilling without Cycles (for example normal to the Surface)

Limits:

  • No Circle Output. If there are Circles into APT-File, these Circles will be linearised by the PP.
  • 2D Cutter compensation not supported.

PP-Output: ToolTip-Coordinates.

 

4.2     Plane Mode

This Mode is used for prismatic Machining on Planes not perpendicular to the axis system (Slope).  If Plane-Mode
is activated, the PP recognize automatic new Planes and set the internal SETPLN-Sequence. So the new Plane
will be activated automatically.  The DEMO PP must be configured for this mode.

Supported in Plane-Mode:

  • Circles
  • 2D Cutter compensation
  • Drilling-Cycles

 

4.3     Manipulation of the Angle-Calculation


Two variants are possible for the Manipulation of the Angle-Calculation (Rotaxis)

In most cases, ANGTWO and SETANG have similar effects.

4.3.1     4.3.1     ANGTWO

Syntax:            ANGTWO

Normally there are more then one Angle-Solution to receive a specific Vector-Position. The PP calculates the shortest Way from the actual position.



If the programmer prefers the second Solution, he can use the PP-Word ANGTWO.


Vector

Basis-Angle

1. Solution

ANGTWO Solution

0.866025,
0.433013,
0.250000

A0 C0


A-60 C60

 

A-120 C-120

 

4.3.2     SETANG

Syntax:            SETANG/<a>, <b>, <c>


With the command SETANG the programmer has influence into the PP-internal Angle-Position.

 

Vector

Angle-Position befor SETANG

SETANG

Angle-Position after SETANG

calculated Angle-Solution

0.866025,
0.433013,
0.250000

A0 C0

SETANG/0,0,0

A0 C0

A-60 C60

A0 C0

SETANG/0,150,0

A0 C150

A120 C120

A0 C0

SETANG/200,0,0

A200 C0

A300 C60

 

If there is a Singularity (Vector 1,0,0), every A-Axis-Position is possible. In this case the SETANG command can define the A-Angle directly. In this case ANGTWO has no effect, because  not only 2 solutions, but also infinite solutions are possible.

 

Vector

Angle-Position befor SETANG

SETANG

Angle-Position after SETANG

calculated Angle-Solution

1,0,0

A0 C0

SETANG/0,0,0

A0 C0

A0 C0

1,0,0

A0 C0

SETANG/77,0,0

A77 C0

A77 C0

1,0,0

A0 C0

SETANG/-77,0,0

A-77 C0

A-77 C0

 

5     ISO Subprogram support

The PP is defined to have the possibility to output each CATIA Machine Operation in a separate ISO subprogram file.  The behaviour is defined with the postprocessor instructions SUBOP/ON which means "SUBprogram per OPeration/ON" and SUBOP/OFF which means  "SUBprogram per OPeration/OFF". Default is "SUBOP/OFF".  The following picture is from the example process for MIK/CE subprogram ISO simulation in the <CATIA Installation>/startup/Manufacturing/CENITCE/Scenarios/MPS_MAKINO_MAG3_ISO_subprogram_simulation:

 

 

The output of ISO subprogram is activated with the PP word SUBOP/ON and the pp will output 7 subprograms for the 7 CATIA machine operations.

6     Drilling cycles

 

 

All  cycles are not supported by this postprocessor parameter file. They can be used in CATIA, but the Output cycle syntax button has to be deactivated.
